<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(true)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeesDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeesDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeesDataView', GridHeight: '600', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeesDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeesDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '600', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeesDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__EmployeesDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeesDataView', GridHeight: '600', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__EmployeesDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__EmployeesDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeesDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeesDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeesDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeesDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__EmployeesDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__EmployeesDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeesDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'EmployeesDataView', GridHeight: '600', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeesDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divEmployeesDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeesDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeesDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeesDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeesDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeesDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__EmployeesDataView').click(function () {

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeesDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeesDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeesDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeesDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeesDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeesDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmployeesDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeesDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeesDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeesDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeesDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__EmployeesDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

<script type="text/javascript">

    function DepartmentChange() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        DepartmentChange(grid);
    }

    $("#btnMassUpdateEmployee__EmployeesDataView").click(function () {

        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

        if (!$("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
            return;

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowMassUpdateEmployee")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassUpdateEmployee" })
                         .SetIsModal(true)
                         .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                         .SetonActivate(function () { RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeMassUpdate", null); })
                         .SetHeight('70%')
                         .SetWidth(900)
                         .SetTitle('Mass Update Employee')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    function EditEmployee(EmployeeId) {

        var id = EmployeeId;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeeFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeeFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        data = { Id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DetailsPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowGoToSource")
               .SetTitle('Edit Employee')
               .SetContent(options)
               .SetWidth('1220')
               .SetHeight('90%')
               .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    }
    function OnPageLoad() {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeesDataView");
        //todo: move to page of grid that was last viewed.
        //RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#EmployeesDataView");

        $("#btnAdd__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CreatePopup", data: {sourceDataView: 'EmployeesDataView' }, type: "POST" };
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowGoToSource")
           .SetTitle('Add Employee')
           .SetContent(options)
           .SetWidth('1220')
           .SetHeight('90%')
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

        });

        $("#btnEdit__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var grid = $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView");
            if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
                var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                EditEmployeeFinsWindow(0, aptaDataViewSelection);

            }

        });

        function DeleteEmployees() {

            var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            //debugger;
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

            $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
                url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MultipleDelete?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (returnData) {
                    NavigateTo("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Search");
                }
            });
        };

        $("#btnDelete__EmployeesDataView").click(function (e) {

            var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeesDataView");

            if (ValidateGridSelection("EmployeesDataView", true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation."))
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected employees", DeleteEmployees);

        });

        function MassApproveJobs() {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/QAAutom/Employee/IsActiveJobInMassApproveSelectedEmployees",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (returnData) {
                    //debugger;
                    if (!returnData) {
                        //redirect to Mass Job approve grid
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob";
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Mass Approve", "One or more of the selected jobs may be part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed. Any changes that have been made to the job(s) will not affect this register. To have the changes apply to the in-process register, the job(s) will have to be removed from the register before running this process. Do you want to continue with the Mass Job Approval?", function () {
                            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob";
                        });
                    }

                },
                error: function (e) {
                    //debugger;
                }
            });

        }

    function ConfirmCalcEmpEvaluations() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
        else {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Calculate Composite Score", "Are you sure you want to calculate evaluations for selected employee(s)?", CalculateEmployeeEvaluations);
        }
    }

    function RefreshOnCalculateEmployeeEvaluations(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var key = "EmployeeSearch";
        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/EvaluationsCalculate',
                     { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, isMultiEmployees: true, operationResultId: massOperationId, key: key },
                '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function CalculateEmployeeEvaluations() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnCalculateEmployeeEvaluations(selectedRowIds); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    function OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd() {

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsNextCycleAvailable',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "No next cycle available for rollover job process.", null);
                    return;
                }

                var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowRolloverEmployeeJob")
                                        .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/RolloverEmployeeJob" }).SetIsModal(true).SetHeight(430).SetWidth(640)
                .SetTitle('Rollover Employee Jobs').SetonDeactivate(function () { UnRegisterActiveScreen(); });
                finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            }
        });

    }

    function ConfirmSetEnabledEmployee(enabled) {
        if (enabled == "True") {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Enable Employee(s)", "Are you sure that you want to enable selected employee(s)? Only disabled employee(s) will be enabled.", EnableEmployees);
        }
        else {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Disable Employee(s)", "Are you sure that you want to disable selected employee(s)? Only enabled employee(s) will be disabled.", DisableEmployees);
        }
    }
    function EnableEmployees()
    { SetEnabledEmployees("True"); }
    function DisableEmployees()
    { SetEnabledEmployees("False"); }
    function SetEnabledEmployees(enabled) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/SetEnabledEmployees?" + "enabled=" + enabled + "&amp;selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (returnData) {
                NavigateTo("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Search");

            }
        });
    }

    $("#btnAdd__EmployeesScreen").click(function (e) {
        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Create";

    });

    $("#btnEdit__EmployeesScreen").click(function (e) {
        if (!$("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        $("#divEmployeesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MultipleEdit",
            dataType: "json",
        success: function (returnData) {
            if (returnData) {
                window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Details/" + returnData.EmployeeId;
            }

        }
    });

    });

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>
    var loadTabJob = true;
    var loadTabAddress = true;
    var loadTabContact = true;
    var loadTabCertificate = true;
    var loadTabLeaves = true;
    var loadExtendedLeave = true;
    var loadTabEducationHistory = true;
    var loadPositionHistory = true;
    var loadEmployeeAttachments = true;
    var loadEmployeeAssignments = true;
    var loadEmployeeElectronicDelivery = true;
    var loadEmployeeAppointments = true;
    var loadEmployeeEvaluations = true;
    var hasApprovedJob = 'False';
    var loadDedcutionAsssignments= true;
    var loadDeductionSetupTab = true;
    function ReturnFromLeave() {

        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '705' };

        $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                var grid = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                if (data.optionalParameters) {
                    $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").SetDataParameters(data.optionalParameters)
                }
                grid.dataSource.one("requestEnd", function () { GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable); });
                grid.dataSource.query({ page: 1, pageSize: grid.dataSource.pageSize(), sort: grid.dataSource.sort(), group: grid.dataSource.group() });
            },
            error: function (e) {
                //
            }
        });
    }
    function ReturnFromAddress() {
        $("#divEmployeeAddressesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
    }

    function ReturnFromContact() {
        $("#divEmployeeContactsDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
    }

    function ReturnFromCertificate() {
        $("#divEmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
    }

    function ReturnFromEducationHistory() {
        $("#divEmployeeEducationHistoryDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();
    }

    }

        $("#divEmployeeEvaluationDataView").data("AptaDataView").Refresh();

    }

    function UpdateDisplayName()
    {
        $("#DisplayName").data("FINSUITextInput").SetValue(($("#LastName").data("FINSUITextInput").Value + ', ' + $("#FirstName").data("FINSUITextInput").Value + ' ' + $("#MiddleName").data("FINSUITextInput").Value));
    }

    function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabStripText = $("#EMPTabStrip").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText()
        if (activeTabStripText == "Addresses") {
            if (loadTabAddress) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAddressesDataView();
                var gridAdd = $("#EmployeeAddressesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabAddress = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAddressesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Deduction Sets') {
            if (loadDedcutionAsssignments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView();
                loadDedcutionAsssignments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeDetailPayrollDeductionAssignmentDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Jobs") {

            if (loadTabJob) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
                var gridAdd = $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabJob = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeJobsDataView");
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == "Contacts") {
            if (loadTabContact) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeContactsDataView();
                var gridContact = $("#EmployeeContactsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabContact = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeContactsDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Certificates") {
            if (loadTabCertificate) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeCertificatesDataView();
                var gridCertificate = $("#EmployeeCertificatesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabCertificate = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeCertificatesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Extended Leave") {
            if (loadExtendedLeave) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView();
                var grid = $("#EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadExtendedLeave = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeExtendedLeavesDataView");
        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Leave Detail") {
            //var gridLeaves = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadTabLeaves) {
                loadTabLeaves = false;
                $('#divEmployeeLeavesDataView').hide();
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail","Employee" , "EmployeeLeavesDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Education History") {
            if (loadTabEducationHistory) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView();
                var grdEducationHistory = $("#EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadTabEducationHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeEducationHistoryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Position History") {
            if (loadPositionHistory) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeePositionHistoryDataView();
                var gridPositionHistory = $("#EmployeePositionHistoryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadPositionHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeePositionHistoryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Attached Files") {
            var gridAttachments = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (loadEmployeeAttachments) {
                loadEmployeeAttachments = false;
                gridAttachments.dataSource.read();
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "Employee", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Assignments") {
            if (loadEmployeeAssignments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAssignmentsDataView();
                var gridAssignments = $("#EmployeeAssignmentsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeAssignments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAssignmentsDataView");

        }
        else if(activeTabStripText == 'Deductions')
        {
            if (loadDeductionSetupTab) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView();
                loadDeductionSetupTab = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeDeductionDetailDataView");
        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Electronic Delivery") {
            if (loadEmployeeElectronicDelivery) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView();
                var gridElectronicDelivery = $("#EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeElectronicDelivery = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeeElectronicDeliveryDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Appointments") {
            if (loadEmployeeAppointments) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeAppointmentsDataView();
                var gridAssignments = $("#EmployeeAppointmentsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeAppointments = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeAppointmentsDataView");

        }
        else if (activeTabStripText == "Evaluations") {
            if (loadEmployeeEvaluations) {
                LoadGridOnDemand__EmployeeEvaluationDataView();
                var gridEvaluations = $("#EmployeeEvaluationDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                loadEmployeeEvaluations = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("EmployeeDetail", "Employee", "EmployeeEvaluationDataView");

        }

    }
</script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").click(function () {

            var Id = $("#hdnMaskedValue_SSNLabel").val();
            var buttonText = $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").text();
            var showValue = buttonText.indexOf("(Show)") &gt; -1;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/QAAutom/AptaFundBase/ShowMaskedValue",
                data: {
                    ControlType: 'SSN', Id: Id, showValue: showValue
                },
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'json',
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                },
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success == true) {
                        if ('SSN' != 'VendorTaxId') {
                            $("#lblSSNValue_SSNLabel").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#lblVendorTaxIdValue_SSNLabel").text(response.Value);
                        }
                        $("#showMaskedValue_SSNLabel").text(response.buttonText);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script>

    $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView")
        .SetFilterColumns('')
        .SetAutoLoad(true)
        .SetEditable(false)

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobsDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeeJobsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobsDataView', GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobsDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeeJobsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeeJobsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeeJobsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#SearchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
        $('#tbFilterName__EmployeeJobsDataView').val("");
        $("#searchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'EmployeeJobsDataView', GridHeight: '300', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobsDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'False',
                selectedRecords: $("#EmployeeJobsDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divEmployeeJobsDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobsDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeeJobsDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobsDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobsDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeeJobsDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ExportToExcel__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("XLS");
    });

    $('#ExportToPdf__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView();
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExportToFile("PDF");
    });

    $('#ClearSearchSettings__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobsDataView()
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearFilterData();
        $('#divOptions__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("padding-top", "0px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("padding-left", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
        $('#divOptions__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("margin-right", "3px");
        $('#divQuickSearch__EmployeeJobsDataView').css("margin-top", "0px");
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobsDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeeJobsDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeeJobsDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeeJobsDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeeJobsDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeeJobsDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobsDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobsDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobsDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeeJobsDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeeJobsDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divEmployeeJobsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

<script>
    function GetLeaveGridData() {
        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '705' };

        //ajax call for grid read on basis of Leave Type Id
        $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
        dataType: "json",
        success: function (data) {
            var grid = $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            if (data.optionalParameters) {
                $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").SetDataParameters(data.optionalParameters)
            }
            grid.dataSource.one("requestEnd", function () { GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable); });
            grid.dataSource.query({ page: 1, pageSize: grid.dataSource.pageSize(), sort: grid.dataSource.sort(), group: grid.dataSource.group() });

            $('#divEmployeeLeavesDataView').show();
        },
        error: function (e) {
            //
        }
    });
    }
</script>

    function ReturnFromPopup__EmployeeLeavesDataView(e) {
        var dataViewSettings = {
            GridHeight: '270',
            AdjustGridHeightOnResize: 'False',
            VerticallyScrollable: 'True',
            IsGridEditable: 'false'
        };

        var urls = {
            ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault',
            ResetNamedGridSettingsSave: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveNamedGridSetting',
            ExistsInSession: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/NamedGridSettingseExistInSession',
            GetGridUserSettingsView: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetUserGridSettingsView',
            GetNamedGridSettings: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetNamedGridSettings',
            DeleteNamedGridSetting: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteNamedGridSetting',
            SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault',
            RemoveMyDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RemoveMyDefault',
            Apply: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyNamedGridSettings'
        };

        var msgs = {
            Success: "Record saved successfully.",
            Delete: "Record deleted successfully.",
            ConfirmDelete: "Confirm Delete",
            DeleteSelectedRecords: "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?"
        };

        UserGridSettingsMenuReturn('/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', e, 'EmployeeLeavesDataView', urls.GetNamedGridSettings, dataViewSettings, urls.Apply,
                                    function (e) {
                                        UserGridSettingsMenuOnSelect(e, '/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'EmployeeLeavesDataView', dataViewSettings, urls, msgs)
                                    });
    }

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeLeavesDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeeLeavesDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeLeavesDataView', GridHeight: '270', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeeLeavesDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeeLeavesDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '270', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeLeavesDataView() {

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeeLeavesDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeLeavesDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeeLeavesDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeLeavesDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeeLeavesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeeLeavesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeeLeavesDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeLeavesDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',

                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divEmployeeLeavesDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeLeavesDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeeLeavesDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeLeavesDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeLeavesDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeeLeavesDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeeLeavesDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'False' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeeLeavesDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeeLeavesDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeeLeavesDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeeLeavesDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeeLeavesDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeLeavesDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeLeavesDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeeLeavesDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeeLeavesDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__EmployeeLeavesDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divEmployeeLeavesDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

<script>

    function EmployeeLeavesDataView__Restore() {
        var leaveTypeId = $('#LeaveTypeId').val();
        var data = { LeaveTypeId: leaveTypeId, EmployeeId: '705' };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/GetLeaveData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                GridLeaveRequestEnd(data.LeaveTaken, data.LeaveAvailable);
            },
            error: function (e) {
                //
            }
        });
    }

    function GridLeaveRequestEnd(LeaveTaken, AvailableLeaves) {

        //update grid header with data
        //debugger;
        var leaveType = $('#LeaveTypeId').data("kendoDropDownList").text();
        if (leaveType === "Personal") {
            $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView thead [data-field=pyEmployeeLeaveTaken__LeaveTaken] .k-link").html("Amount (Hours)");
        }
        else {
            $("#EmployeeLeavesDataView thead [data-field=pyEmployeeLeaveTaken__LeaveTaken] .k-link").html("Amount (Days)");
        }

        var Taken = 'Leave Taken: ' + LeaveTaken;
        var Available = 'Available Leave: ' + AvailableLeaves;

        setTimeout(function () { showFooterText(Taken, Available); }, 900);
    }

    function showFooterText(LeaveTaken, LeaveAvailable) {
        $('#LeaveTaken__Footer').text(LeaveTaken);
        $('#LeaveComment__Footer').text(LeaveAvailable);
    }

    function IsEmployeeInPayroll() {
                    var ddlLeaveTypeId = $("#LeaveTypeId").data("kendoDropDownList");
                            ddlLeaveTypeId.enable(false);
                            $('#btnAdd__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                            $('#btnEdit__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                            $('#btnDelete__EmployeeLeavesDataView').unbind('click');
                    $('#divFormEmployeeLeaveErrors').html("Leave information cannot be displayed if employee is disabled or not yet submitted to payroll.");
                            $('#divFormEmployeeLeaveErrors').addClass("global_message notice");
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        IsEmployeeInPayroll();
    });
</script>

<script>

	$(document).ready(function () {
        function ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement() {
            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            grid.dataSource.read();
            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        }

        $("#btnAdd__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__EmployeeManagement")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/AddAttachment?ScreenName=EmployeeManagement" + "&amp;ObjectKey1=705" + "&amp;ObjectKey2=-1" + "&amp;ObjectKey3=" })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement)
                      .SetTitle("Add Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__EmployeeManagement", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");
        });

        $("#btnEdit__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
            }

            var gridData = grid.dataSource.data();
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; gridData.length; i++) {
                if (gridData[i].Id == selectedRowIds &amp;&amp; gridData[i].syViewFileAttachments__ScreenName != 'EmployeeManagement') {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Linked attachment cannot be edited", "error");
                    return;
                }
            }

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAttachmentFramework__EmployeeManagement")
                      .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/EditAttachment?FileId=" + selectedRowIds })
                      .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromAttachmentPopup__EmployeeManagement)
                      .SetTitle("Edit Attachment")
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "frmAttachment__EmployeeManagement", "AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement");
        });

        $("#btnDelete__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {
            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
                ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Delete', 'Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?', DeleteAttachments);
            }
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }
        });

        function DeleteAttachments() {
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(MassActionResultRefresh).
    SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        }

        function MassActionResultRefresh()
        {
            var massActionId = GetMassActionId();
            $("#divAttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteAttachment',
				{ massOpertaionId: massActionId, dataView: "AttachmentFrameworkDataView" },
                    '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        //removing selection from the attributes.
                        grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                        grid.thead.find("tr .selectAll__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").attr("checked", false);
                        SetGridSelectedRecords("AttachmentFrameworkDataView", "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        //refresh grid
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
        }

        $("#btnView__AttachmentFrameworkDataView__EmployeeManagement").click(function () {

            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
			}
			window.location.href = "/QAAutom/GridConfig/ViewAttachment" + "?dataView=AttachmentFrameworkDataView";

        });

    });
</script>

    function ReturnFromPopup__AttachmentFrameworkDataView(e) {
        var dataViewSettings = {
            GridHeight: '300',
            AdjustGridHeightOnResize: 'False',
            VerticallyScrollable: 'False',
            IsGridEditable: 'false'
        };

        var urls = {
            ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ResetNamedGridSettingsToDefault',
            ResetNamedGridSettingsSave: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveNamedGridSetting',
            ExistsInSession: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/NamedGridSettingseExistInSession',
            GetGridUserSettingsView: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetUserGridSettingsView',
            GetNamedGridSettings: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetNamedGridSettings',
            DeleteNamedGridSetting: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/DeleteNamedGridSetting',
            SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetNamedGridSettingAsDefault',
            RemoveMyDefault: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RemoveMyDefault',
            Apply: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyNamedGridSettings'
        };

        var msgs = {
            Success: "Record saved successfully.",
            Delete: "Record deleted successfully.",
            ConfirmDelete: "Confirm Delete",
            DeleteSelectedRecords: "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?"
        };

        UserGridSettingsMenuReturn('/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', e, 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', urls.GetNamedGridSettings, dataViewSettings, urls.Apply,
                                    function (e) {
                                        UserGridSettingsMenuOnSelect(e, '/Content/Images/filtericons/Gear.png', 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', dataViewSettings, urls, msgs)
                                    });
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__AttachmentFrameworkDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataView() {

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView', GridHeight: '300', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AttachmentFrameworkDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'False',
                selectedRecords: $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divAttachmentFrameworkDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___AttachmentFrameworkDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AttachmentFrameworkDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "AttachmentFrameworkDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("AttachmentFrameworkDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___AttachmentFrameworkDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("AttachmentFrameworkDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__AttachmentFrameworkDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__AttachmentFrameworkDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__AttachmentFrameworkDataView() {
        var gridName = 'AttachmentFrameworkDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___AttachmentFrameworkDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AttachmentFrameworkDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "AttachmentFrameworkDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_AttachmentFrameworkDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__AttachmentFrameworkDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__AttachmentFrameworkDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divAttachmentFrameworkDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });
